Italy-Abyssinia Peace Talks Revised Conditions: Abyssinia Still Expresses Rejection, and Asks the League of Nations to Intensify Sanctions Against Italy. The Thirteen-Nation Committee's Mediation is Ineffective.

(Geneva) Abyssinia, due to Italy's refusal to negotiate peace within the League of Nations framework, has appealed to the League of Nations to implement various sanctions under Article 16 of the League Covenant. Today, the Abyssinian representative firmly rejected the peace terms proposed by Italy and notified the thirteen-nation committee, declaring this point. According to Italy's conditions: Italy does not allow the League of Nations to participate in negotiations; Italy does not want to submit its treaty terms to the League of Nations, but only to Abyssinia, treating it as negotiations between victor and vanquished; Italy does not allow a ceasefire. The chairman of the thirteen-nation committee, Madariaga, met with the Italian representative this afternoon to obtain a detailed report to convey to the other committee members. After Abyssinia rejected Italy's peace proposal, Madariaga immediately asked the Italian representative, Aloisi, to revise his conditions. Aloisi, after consulting with Rome, has agreed to make slight revisions, allowing League of Nations observers to participate in the negotiations, or to notify the League of Nations of the progress of the negotiations. The thirteen-nation committee has now decided to convey this revised plan to the Abyssinian representative. However, judging from the tone of Abyssinia's first letter, this revised plan will be rejected by Abyssinia. The thirteen-nation committee is now adjourned until 4 p.m. tomorrow. If Abyssinia does reject it, then the thirteen-nation committee can only record that reconciliation has failed. Then the eighteen-nation committee must be convened to consider intensifying sanctions against Italy. Abyssinia's letter asks the thirteen-nation committee to note that Italy refuses to engage in negotiations within the League of Nations structure in the spirit of the League of Nations, and states that the time has come for the implementation of various sanctions stipulated in Article 16 of the Covenant and the fulfillment of various obligations undertaken by League members. League member states have an obligation to immediately assist the invaded country in an effective manner. The people of Abyssinia are now facing the disaster of annihilation. The Abyssinian government, in this most urgent moment, does not want to hastily believe that Abyssinia cannot obtain this protection. (Reuters, November 11)

(Geneva) After the preliminary peace terms proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini were rejected by Abyssinia, the chairman of the thirteen-nation committee, Madariaga, and the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, advised the Abyssinian representative, Wolde, this morning to reconsider them. Wolde has again expressed his rejection. As for French Minister Without Portfolio, Penancier, he agreed with the Italian representative, Aloisi's proposal to immediately cease hostilities. Aloisi has not yet provided an answer. The thirteen-nation committee is scheduled to hold a meeting at 4 p.m. Its mediation efforts have effectively failed. (Havas, November 17)

(Geneva) It is widely expected that the thirteen-nation committee's meeting at 4 p.m. today will determine whether there is any hope of bringing Italy and Abyssinia closer together. This meeting must record the success or failure of peace efforts. If reconciliation fails, then this committee must report to the League of Nations Sanctions Committee, i.e., the eighteen-nation committee. But at present, there are no arrangements for the eighteen-nation committee to meet. (Reuters, November 17)

France Asks Italy for a Truce

Italian Representative Asks Mussolini for Instructions

(Geneva) France has now asked Italy to declare a truce to prevent the failure of the thirteen-nation committee's reconciliation efforts. After the Abyssinian representative rejected Italy's revised conditions and declared that all negotiations must not go beyond the League of Nations framework and must not violate the spirit of the Covenant, French Minister Penancier went to see the Italian representative, Aloisi, saying that if Italy could officially announce a truce, even for a few days, so that the current peace talks have a chance of success, this would be a most welcome gesture. Aloisi replied that there are strategically important operations currently underway in East Africa, and this French proposal is unlikely to be adopted. However, he is willing to discuss this matter with Mussolini in Italy. (Reuters, November 17)

(Geneva) Regarding the issue of peace between Italy and Abyssinia, French Minister Without Portfolio, Penancier, met with the Italian representative, Aloisi, this morning and suggested to him that Italy should immediately agree to a truce. This will certainly have a great impact in the current situation and will facilitate the negotiations currently being conducted by the thirteen-nation committee. Aloisi replied that he would ask his government for instructions, but Prime Minister Mussolini is unlikely to accept this proposal. (Havas, November 17)

(Geneva) After French Minister Without Portfolio, Penancier, met with the Italian representative, Aloisi, this morning, he then met with the British Foreign Secretary, Eden. Eden then also met with the Abyssinian representative, i.e., the Abyssinian envoy to France, Wolde, and the chairman of the League of Nations eighteen-nation committee, i.e., the Portuguese representative, Vasco-Concelos. (Havas, November 17)

(London) According to responsible sources, regarding the issue of peace between Italy and Abyssinia, any negotiation procedure that goes beyond the scope of the League of Nations is opposed by Britain. It is currently believed here that the only hope for improving the peace situation is for Italy to agree to revise the conditions it has proposed. If Italy refuses to revise them, then the current sanctions measures should continue to be implemented. These sources still advocate that the League of Nations General Assembly's eighteen-nation sub-committee should be convened immediately to study the issue of intensifying sanctions against Italy. (Havas, November 16)

(Geneva) After the meeting of the League of Nations Administrative Council's thirteen-nation committee today, the spokesman for the French delegation immediately declared that an agreement between Italy and Abyssinia has not been despaired of. However, reporters from this agency have learned that the views of the British are the opposite of those of the French, and they advocate intensifying sanctions against Italy, saying that the thirteen-nation committee's compromise work is a failure. The committee will make a clear announcement after its meeting tomorrow. (Havas, November 16)

Italy's Peace Terms

Official Terms Submitted Directly to Abyssinia; Meetings Must Be Held Outside of Geneva; Ceasefire to Be Negotiated by Frontline Generals

(Geneva) Regarding the terms of the preliminary peace proposal put forward by Italy, reporters from this agency have learned from the Italian delegation that Italy believes that future peace negotiations can be held in a city near Geneva, such as Ouchy on Lake Geneva, as an example. However, it opposes holding them directly in Geneva. Furthermore, these negotiations should be held directly between the two parties involved. As for the League of Nations' position, the Italian government initially maintained that it would only notify it with a document after the negotiations had achieved results. Later, due to the strong requests of French Minister Without Portfolio, Penancier, British Foreign Secretary, Eden, the chairman of the thirteen-nation committee, Madariaga, and the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, Aloisi obtained instructions from his government via long-distance telephone, agreeing to "constantly notify" the thirteen-nation committee of the progress of the negotiations during the negotiation period. The two parties involved can also submit applications to the committee at any time. However, Italy can only submit the peace terms to Abyssinia, and it will not notify the League of Nations. The thirteen-nation committee has no objection to this, because the committee can "constantly contact" Italy and Abyssinia. After Abyssinia receives Italy's peace terms, it will naturally notify the committee. Regarding the issue of a ceasefire, the Italian government has stated that either the two sides can negotiate a ceasefire agreement, or they can negotiate preliminary articles of peace. One of the two must be chosen. However, if a ceasefire agreement is signed, then military action should cease immediately. Therefore, the demands that Italy can make must be very significant. According to Aloisi's view, it is more appropriate to negotiate a preliminary treaty at this time. (Havas, November 16) Italy has recently proposed the conditions of a "preliminary peace," the content of which is divided into two items: 1. The military authorities of Italy and Abyssinia should negotiate on the spot regarding ceasefire measures. The indigenous tribes of Abyssinia should disarm under the supervision of the Italian army to ensure the safety of the Italian army. 2. The negotiations for the "final peace" will be held by plenipotentiary representatives from the two countries at a location outside of Geneva. The League of Nations may send observers to attend the meeting, but may not directly interfere in the negotiations. It must wait until the negotiations fail, or for the sake of approving the future agreement, before it can come forward to intervene. The Abyssinian delegation has recently sent a note to the chairman of the thirteen-nation committee, Madariaga, expressing strong protests, saying that "the Italian government is nothing more than speculating and demanding high prices, as if to say that if the League of Nations can withdraw the sanctions measures and stay out of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, then Italy can help the League of Nations once something happens in Europe. The procedure it suggests, if implemented, will inevitably set a bad precedent and make the fate of small countries precarious, which the Abyssinian government cannot accept." It also said that what Abyssinia seeks is nothing more than the implementation of the basic principles of the League of Nations Covenant, which is also what the French memorandum of April 8 (regarding the Locarno case) has repeatedly stated. It is time for the various agencies of the League of Nations to take responsibility. (Havas, November 16)

(Geneva) Italy today proposed conditions for peace with Abyssinia, advocating that before the negotiations, Abyssinia should first negotiate directly with the commander of the Italian army in East Africa, Badoglio Rivoli. Aloisi, the Italian representative to the League of Nations, insisted that the East African War should be based on the precedent of the European War, and that the general staff of the two warring countries should sign a ceasefire agreement. Therefore, the peace work of the thirteen-nation committee has almost completely stalled. The Italian representative also notified the League of Nations leaders that after this direct negotiation begins, Italy is prepared to negotiate peace terms in Ouchy, Switzerland. Italy allows the progress of future negotiations to be notified to the thirteen-nation committee, but the League of Nations itself does not need to participate, and the League of Nations must guarantee that Abyssinia will not counterattack after Italy's ceasefire. Today, Abyssinia's envoy to France and representative to the League of Nations, Mariam, and the French representative, Qi Qi, have rejected Italy's conditions in the name of the Abyssinian government. The thirteen-nation committee then held a secret meeting in the evening to listen to Chairman Madariaga's report on the peace work. (National News Agency, November 16)

Thirteen-Nation Committee Meeting Held in Secret

Continues to Mediate Between Italy and Abyssinia

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council's thirteen-nation committee met at 6:15 p.m. today to discuss the issue of peace between Italy and Abyssinia, ending at 7:45 p.m. The process was extremely secret. Afterwards, a public report will be issued by the League of Nations Secretariat stating that negotiations are still in progress, and stating that "the chairman of the thirteen-nation committee, Madariaga, and the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, held talks with the Italian delegation this afternoon, and the results obtained will naturally be notified to the Abyssinian delegation. The committee is now scheduled to continue its meeting at 4 p.m. on Friday (i.e., November 17)." It is generally known that Madariaga has requested supplementary explanations from the Italian representative, Aloisi, regarding Italy's peace terms, and is now waiting for Mr. Aloisi's reply. (Havas, November 16)

(Geneva) The meeting of the thirteen-nation committee today was extremely secret. Each national representative was only allowed to bring one assistant. At the meeting, the representatives of various countries mostly expressed their views, wishing to see an early end to the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. It is heard that British Foreign Secretary Eden and Administrative Council Chairman Bruce (Australian representative) also expressed their willingness to compromise, and Bruce's wording was particularly moderate, which was praised by the representatives of various countries after the meeting. As for the French representative, Penancier, he explained that the cessation of hostilities between Italy and Abyssinia is the ideal of the League of Nations. This is what France is eagerly seeking, so that Italy can re-engage actively in European affairs. The committee finally decided that Chairman Madariaga and Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, should notify the Abyssinian delegation tonight that after the committee contacted the Italian representative, Aloisi, the prospects for peace are more optimistic, and that the Abyssinian representative should reconsider the situation, or revise the first note it submitted (i.e., the note protesting against Italy's conditions). However, it is generally believed that the views of the two parties involved, Italy and Abyssinia, are still divergent, and it is feared that it will still be difficult to reconcile them. (Havas, November 16)

(Geneva) The Abyssinian delegation, after conducting talks with the chairman of the thirteen-nation committee, Madariaga, and the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, at 11 a.m. this morning, issued a statement saying that Abyssinia still opposes the preliminary peace terms proposed by Italy. As for the request by Madariaga and Avenol to reconsider them, a reply will be submitted, and it will be sent to the thirteen-nation committee in a short period of time. The thirteen-nation committee is scheduled to continue its meeting at 4 p.m. today. (Havas, November 17)

(Paris) Regarding the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, the famous journalist Madame Tabouis recently published a commentary in the "L'Oeuvre" newspaper, saying, "Britain has not yet decided whether to impose military sanctions on Italy. As for Sir Drummond, the British ambassador to Italy, he reported to the Italian Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday that although the rainy season in Abyssinia has begun, the road from the front line directly to the Abyssinian capital has been controlled by the Italian army. The motorized units of the Italian army can drive straight in within a few days without any obstacles. Fortunately, the morale of the Abyssinian army is still strong. Even if the capital falls, they can continue to fight without surrendering. As for Italy, due to economic hardship, it is necessary to cease hostilities immediately, because the country currently has to spend huge military expenses, and after the victory, it must also pacify the region, which will also cost a lot. Its predicament is obvious. From the British point of view, Italy, after this war, will eventually feel exhausted economically, financially, and militarily. In the future, its attitude towards colonial and European issues will inevitably be more compromising." (Havas, November 17)

Two Italian Aircraft Launch Rockets Over Abyssinian Capital

Colors Matched to Form the Italian National Flag; A Novel Way to Indicate Occupation

(London) According to a report from a correspondent in Cairo received by The Times, the Abyssinian Northern Army is now in a state of total collapse. Unless the rainy season arrives immediately to prevent the advance of the Italian air force, the Abyssinian army has no hope of recovery. According to what the correspondent knows, the main reason for the defeat of the Abyssinian Northern Army is that the Gala warriors of the country have been incited by the Italian army to betray the Abyssinian Emperor. At the beginning of last month, the Italian and Abyssinian armies were deadlocked in the Emba Aratchi area, which is an important area on the northern front and can be defended. However, the Gala warriors retreated without fighting, causing the Guards Brigade to retreat with them. The Abyssinian Emperor had no choice but to deploy defenses near Lake Ashenge in an attempt to contain the enemy. Unfortunately, the terrain there is far inferior to Emba Aratchi. The Italian army was able to take advantage of the victory and advance south, as if splitting bamboo. (Havas, November 17)

(Rome) The General Headquarters announced today that the Italian army in Abyssinia continues to advance south towards the Sudanese border, so it has gradually moved away from areas related to Britain's vital interests. The most recent target of attack will be Boni. After the Italian army occupies the area, it can expand its control and extend it to the camel trails and the Rahal River, a tributary of the Nile. After this, it will attack the Zaré and other bottlenecks of the camel trails connecting Lake Chana to Sudan. Although the Italians are extremely concerned about military affairs, they are not concerned about the policies in Geneva. According to recent rumors, General Badoglio, the commander of the Italian army in East Africa, will be stationed in the Abyssinian capital in May. The Italian army may be able to enter the Abyssinian capital within a week, because the road to the Abyssinian capital is flat and wide, which is conducive to the movement of military vehicles. The military here does not believe the claim that the Italian army has already begun to attack the Abyssinian capital, because the Italian army in Tessenei is mostly infantry. It is said that General Badoglio will first attack east and link up with the Italian army departing from Sardo and passing through the Danakil area, and then flank Harar. General Graziani will then launch an attack from the south to meet them. (National News Agency, November 16)

Italian Army Bombs British Medical Team; Britain Lodges Strong Protest

Believes It Was Deliberately Provoked

(Geneva) According to the League of Nations news released today, the British Ambassador to Italy, Drummond, sent a strongly worded official document to the Italian government, protesting against the repeated bombing of the British Red Cross medical team by Italian aircraft, saying that in March, the British medical team in Guarani, Abyssinia, was bombed by Italian aircraft for four consecutive days without any interruption. The Italian representative claimed that the medical team members had shot at the bombers, and that the planes were retaliating. After a detailed investigation by the British government, this statement was found to be untrue and cannot be admitted. According to the report of the chief physician, there is no doubt that the Italian aircraft deliberately provoked the situation. The British government believes that the remarks and memoranda issued by Soviet Vice-Premier Zhu are nothing more than responsible personnel trying to find excuses to cover up their bombing of the British medical team. Britain is now demanding that the Italian government make a firm statement, ordering the Italian air force to be extra cautious in the future and not to attack the British Red Cross and medical teams in Abyssinia. Bank of France Gold Reserves Decrease Again

(Paris) The Bank of France recently released its weekly report (April 3 to April 10). On the asset side, cash reserves decreased by 945,000,000 francs (compared to the previous two weeks, from March 20 to April 3, gold reserves had already decreased by 2,615,000,000 francs). In addition, the total amount of discounted bills increased by 239,000,000 francs due to the approaching closing date of April 15. Securities-backed loans decreased by 65,000,000 francs. Short-term loans secured by government bonds decreased by 294,000,000 francs. On the liability side, the amount of banknotes in circulation decreased by 740,000,000 francs, and deposits decreased by 118,000,000 francs, totaling a decrease of 858,000,000 francs. The banknote reserve ratio decreased from 67.42 percent to 67.03 percent. (Havas, April 16)

(Paris) The Radical Socialist Party, i.e., the current government party, recently issued an appeal to the people of the country, asking voters nationwide to uphold "freedom, economic revival, and peace." It said, "For the past year or two, the Bank of France, in order to stop malicious propaganda aimed at undermining the French currency, has implemented a large-scale contraction policy in a systematic manner, but it has still failed to meet expectations. As a result, the amount that the Treasury should spend this year is as high as 16,000,000,000 francs, and the amount of gold flowing out of the country has reached a huge sum of 10,000,000,000 francs. What our party seeks is to earnestly safeguard the revival of the franc, revive the economy, protect the democratic rights of the people, and achieve the goal of limiting and reducing armaments based on collective security and mutual assistance systems, thereby realizing true and lasting peace. In addition, our party should safeguard the middle class, i.e., the foundation of France, agriculture, and the honest and sound working class to resist parasitic feudal forces and prevent them from monopolizing the banking system, controlling prices, and monopolizing goods, while allowing the middle class to bear the responsibility for mistakes." (Havas, April 17)

More than Ten Casualties in Left-Right Conflicts; Traffic in the Capital Severed, Pedestrians Vanished

Madrid: Members of the General Confederation of Labor are currently distributing leaflets in the streets, stating that a general strike has been announced and is in effect, without specifying a time limit. The general public believes that work will resume on the first of next week. (Havas, 17th)

Trams, buses, trains, and subways have all stopped. All shops, except for milk shops and pharmacies, have also closed. There are hardly any pedestrians on the streets. As of noon, no major incidents have occurred. (Havas, 17th)

The military and police immediately searched for Fascists and those suspected of causing trouble. As of now, it is reported that as many as a thousand people have been arrested. The left-wing People's Front has also organized special teams to patrol the streets to prevent "Fascist provocative behavior." In addition, security team members are stationed everywhere and will search anyone who looks suspicious at any time. Various labor unions and Communist and Socialist Party organizations in the capital are separately informing their members to pay attention to the development of the situation so that they can adapt to the situation. It is also reported that various labor organizations are deeply dissatisfied with the Fascist Party's recent repeated insults to left-wing individuals and the fact that security team members also lined up to participate in Lieutenant Rifles' funeral, and plan to announce a general strike to protest. Trends in the U.S. Presidential Election: Democrats Very Optimistic

Republican Candidates Vie for Nomination

(Washington) Democratic leaders today generally stated that the current primary results are sufficient to be considered an omen of government victory in this autumn's presidential election. The Republican side has made no comments. President Roosevelt's vote counts in Wisconsin, Illinois, and Nebraska all exceeded those of the Republican Party, and no one in the party is competing with him. Some observers firmly believe that Senator Borah's ability to achieve his current results in Illinois, despite being under strong opposition, is truly commendable. Chicago publisher Knox also failed to achieve a major victory, so experts believe that Knox and Borah are in a "clam and snipe" fight, only benefiting Kansas Governor Landon. Landon has not yet made any comments, but yesterday's primary results in Nebraska showed Roosevelt receiving 79,354 votes, Borah 62,420 votes, and Landon 61,472 votes. Supporters of Landon say that since Landon was not listed as a candidate, having so many votes indicates that with a little organization, he could obtain all of Borah's votes. Most experts believe that Landon is the most promising Republican candidate, followed perhaps by Senator Vandenberg. People on Landon's side claim that Landon can get 472 votes at the Republican National Convention. If so, he would be only 27 votes short of the majority needed to become the candidate. (National Telegram, 16th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt today laid the cornerstone for the new $12 million building of the Department of the Interior and gave a speech advocating for the preservation of national resources. The trowel used by the President to lay the cornerstone was the same one used by President Washington in 1793 to lay the cornerstone for the U.S. Capitol. President Roosevelt declared that national resources, if not abundant and without policies for their preservation, would have ceased to exist long ago. It is truly astonishing that we have been developing, wasting, and misappropriating the resources of all mankind for so long and still do not find it strange. We should strive now to ensure that those who come after us can enjoy the benefits they deserve. (National Telegram, 16th)

Reuters Special Business Telegram, April 17

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price: Today is 140 shillings.

Mount Lyell Silver: Firm today due to the entry of peers and speculators. The July futures price at the start of trading was 46.36-47.50, up 31 pounds from yesterday's closing.

The opening exchange rate for sterling-dollar was $4.9425, down .025 from yesterday's close in the US-British market, but rose .0625 an hour later to $4.943125. This price was unchanged at 1:00 PM.

Cotton and Wheat: New York Cotton Market: The opening was firm due to industry purchases. The July futures price rose 3 points in the first half hour to 11.09. The market was stable later but lacked excitement. The price was unchanged at 11:00 AM.

Liverpool Cotton: US cotton futures were stable today. The May futures price at 1:00 PM was 6.6, up 1 point from the closing.

Chicago Wheat: This morning, due to weather news favorable to the bulls, speculative buying was triggered, so the market price rose sharply. A few minutes after the opening, the July futures price was 9.25, up one point from yesterday's close. The price continued to rise at 11:00 AM due to active trading, up .75 from yesterday's close. The market for miscellaneous grains was firm, and prices moved with the rise and fall of wheat prices.

Liverpool Linseed: The opening today was stable. Although the market prices in Chicago and Winnipeg were low, and there were reports of yesterday's rainfall in the wheat-growing region, the market here was not affected at the start of trading due to Italy's purchase of a batch of Australian wheat. Later, the market became increasingly firm due to the small amount of visible inventory in Australia, which was beneficial to the bulls, and the small number of weekly shipments. The price of the May futures contract at 11:00 AM was 6 shillings, 1 penny, 875, up half a penny.

Rubber: London: The market was quiet and lacked excitement today. The closing price for July and September at 1:00 PM was 7 pence 6875, the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York: Futures were quiet and lacked excitement this morning. The July futures price fell 1 point to 16.16. The market price stabilized at 11:00 AM and did not continue to fall. The market prices of goods in New York are listed on the left.

South Manchuria Railway to Control North China Transportation

Operating Nine Automobile Routes Within the War Zone

Interconnecting with the Pseudo-Jehol Railway

Planning to Establish a Commercial Port at Dalingkou

Tianjin Communication: The North China economic development being carried out by the Japanese Garrison Headquarters in Tianjin in conjunction with the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) has become a mutually supportive strategy. Although the Japanese military's economic advisory department (also known as the General Staff Headquarters) seems to be developing plans independently, separate from military affairs, its ultimate goal is still to support future military convenience. The economic development methods formulated by Mantetsu, such as building the Cangshi Road, mining the Longyan iron and coal mines, and building a steel mill in Tangshan, Pingxi, are also intended to supply future military needs. In the middle of last month, Ishimoto Kenji, the Mantetsu representative in Tianjin, convened a meeting in Tianjin to organize the materials from the first stage of the investigation and summarize the proposals from representatives stationed in various places. He then took them back to Dalian to present to Matsuoka Yosuke, the president of Mantetsu. Recently, Matsuoka convened a special meeting for this purpose, which was attended by representatives from Mantetsu offices in North China. Even before its resolutions have been implemented, it has been decided to first complete the automobile transportation network between the war zone, the Great Wall passes, and Tianjin and Beijing, as a starting point for future economic development. It is planned to establish the North China Automobile Transportation Company within the Tianjin office, with the Tianjin office director Ota Masao concurrently serving as director. The designated automobile routes are nine: Shanhaiguan to Jianchangying, Tangshan to Xifengkou, Duolun to Zhangjiakou, Beiping to Chengde, Luanxian to Leting, Tianjin to Tangshan, Tianjin to Tanggu, Tianjin to Beiping, Beiping to Zhangjiakou. Of the above nine routes, the Shanhaiguan to Jianchangying route has always been operated by the Shan-Jian Automobile Transportation Company, established by the pseudo-Manchukuo Railway Bureau. The Tangshan to Xifengkou route and the Zhangjiakou to Duolun route are operated by the Mingxin Automobile Transportation Company and the Zhang-Duo Automobile Transportation Company, respectively, established by the International Transportation Company. The Beiping to Chengde route has been operated by the Pingcheng Automobile Company organized by Sakata. All of the above routes were purchased separately by Mantetsu on April 10th and contracts were signed. From now on, the business of long-distance automobiles within the so-called war zone, south of the Great Wall, and north of Tianjin and Beijing will be entirely operated by the newly established North China Automobile Transportation Company in Tianjin. The company will purchase one hundred passenger and freight automobiles and connect with the Yechi, Jin-Chao railways, and Cheng-Gu automobile road within the territory of Rehe. The capital is set at 500,000 yuan. The automobile roads traversed will be built by the Mantetsu-assisted Construction Department of the pseudo-Hebei-East Autonomous Anti-Communist Council. The goal is to control North China's transportation within six months, and at its core, it has more subtle and mysterious connections to military affairs. In January, the Naval Ministry planned to build a military and commercial port at the mouth of the Luan River in Eastern Hebei. This plan has now become a thing of the past, but recently, the pseudo-Hebei-East government has proposed to open Leting Daling River mouth as a commercial port. The construction costs are borrowed from the Mantetsu company, and the construction is scheduled for five years, to be managed by the Construction Department of the pseudo-Hebei-East government, which will hire Japanese engineers from Mantetsu to design it. According to the pseudo-government's own claims, the motivation for building the port is that there are no good commercial ports in eastern Luan, and Tanggu and Qinhuangdao are both too narrow and are subject to annual freezing. This year's ice blockage, for example, has disrupted ship traffic and caused severe losses. The Daling River has been inspected and surveyed by Chinese and foreign personnel and is better than the ports of Qin and Tang. In the past, the Zhili Provincial Assembly planned to build a wharf there, 24 li into the sea, where the largest European and American ships could dock and berth directly, and lay a railway directly from the port to the Rehe Railway. Goods brought in by ship could be unloaded there and loaded onto trains, and goods transported by train could be loaded onto ships and transported abroad. It was estimated to cost more than 75 million yuan, with the port and road projects proceeding simultaneously. Later, due to political changes, it was not realized. Dr. Sun Yat-sen also designated the area as one of the three major good ports in the north and established the Northern Great Port Preparatory Office to conduct climate measurements, test warm currents, and survey routes. The pseudo-Hebei-East government does not have the ability to open the port, but it is actually planning to proceed with it, so the subtle relationship is self-evident. (14th)

Serious Spring Famine in Hua County, Henan; Poor People Rise Up to Seize and Distribute Grain

Kaifeng Communication: Hua County has suffered years of drought and flooding, and the crops have failed. The lives of farmers are difficult, and they have reached the extreme. The spring famine is especially severe this year. Most of the food supplies rely on external sources, but these are hoarded by speculators at the Wangzhuang Railway Station. Local rich farmers have also buried all of their surplus grain, making the food problem even more dire. Traitors are taking the opportunity to incite people, calling for "everyone to share the food." As a result, grain seizures have occurred. It started in the Wadian Town of the Eighth District, where more than 800 poor people occupied the Fuxing Temple outside the north gate of the town, guarded the gate, and prohibited entry and exit. Their momentum was fierce, and they declared their intention to seize grain. After persuasion by the joint security director of the town, gentry merchants and wealthy households collected more than 2,000 yuan to establish a porridge kitchen and provide meals immediately, and the disturbance subsided. However, incidents followed in Cizhouzhai, Jiaoguangji, Tunjiaji, Yangzhao, and other places. Now, in the Fourth, Fifth, Sixth, Seventh, and Eighth Districts, there are almost no villages without them. There is a tendency for it to spread throughout the county. (15th)

Private Banknotes in Xianyou, Southern Fujian, Cease Redemption; More Than 300,000 Yuan Affected

Mostly Held by Farmers

Xiamen Communication: The currency used in Xianyou County, which belongs to southern Fujian Xinghua district, is mostly paper money privately issued by merchants, called "Jiao Piao." The businesses that issue these banknotes are called "Piao Ju." Since the 15th year of the Republic (1926), "Piao Ju" have been opened and have issued banknotes, but mostly with the aim of collecting money and profiting by purchasing longan agricultural products and sugar from farmers with paper money. Therefore, some have capital of only a few thousand yuan but issue banknotes worth tens of thousands of yuan. In the 18th year of the Republic (1929), all Piao Ju were once cancelled, and the Tongyi Piao Ju was jointly established by various merchant guilds to issue banknotes. By the 22nd year of the Republic (1933), other Piao Ju sprung up like bamboo shoots after a rain, but they collapsed in less than a year, leaving only Tongyi Piao Ju. The abandoned banknotes from the bankrupt banks flowed into the hands of the people and have not yet been redeemed. According to the investigation, Xuanlong owed 81,771 yuan, Xinyi 41,803 yuan, Xiandong 17,054 yuan, Limin 7,865 yuan, Xianyi 2,742 yuan, Tonghe 4,126 yuan, Fuxiang 1,161 yuan, Minyou 468 yuan, Fengmei 1,227 yuan, totaling 158,217 yuan. The losses suffered by farmers have been extremely severe. Unexpectedly, Tongyi Piao Ju also went bankrupt at the end of last year. For a time, there was almost no currency in circulation in the entire county, which almost caused a major disturbance. Although the county government arrested Chen Feiting, the chairman of the bank, and strictly ordered him to find a way to redeem the banknotes, due to a lack of funds, only over a thousand yuan of 2-jiao banknotes have been redeemed to date. According to the bank's liquidation report, as of March 23, the banknotes issued and circulating among the people that have not been redeemed include 17,710 yuan in 5-yuan notes, 82,193 yuan in 1-yuan notes, 38,584 yuan in 5-jiao notes, and 3,080 yuan in 1-jiao notes, totaling 151,567 yuan. There is currently no concrete plan for redemption. Including the unredeemed jiao banknotes from the already bankrupt banks, the total reaches more than 300,000 yuan, mostly in the hands of farmers. (April 13)

Xinjiang Women Highly Value Chastity

Ma Si-Wu-De Writes Article Offering True Introduction

Beijing News: Since a Xinjiang dispatch was published containing erroneous information about the issue of chastity among Xinjiang women, Hui Muslims in various places have been extremely indignant. Two newspapers in Beiping were even vandalized, causing disputes. Mai Si-Wu-De, a member of the Central Committee from Xinjiang, who is currently in Beijing, recently wrote a special article introducing the issue of chastity among Xinjiang women, entitled "A Mother's Most Sacred Responsibility." The original text is excerpted below:

Mothers Protect Their Daughters' Chastity

In Xinjiang, the most sacred and most important responsibility that mothers shoulder, is to protect the chastity of their daughters. Proof of such chastity lies in the hymen. To meet this responsibilty, pitiful mothers devote countless methods toward that goal. Daughters, precious as their own hearts, are prohibited from any strenuous activities once they reach the age of 12. Even seemingly innocuous things such as skipping and jumping are meticulously guarded against. The honour, glory and shame of their families and their races are fully entrusted upon their daughters. They have faith in and work hard at these methods. Some points are embarrassing to speak of, but I must bring them up. On the very day of the wedding celebrations, all people are filled with the highest of spirits, but the mothers display a somber air of worry. Their worries are triggered by the fear that their daughters' virginity might be found to be lacking, which would bring immense shame upon their families and their race. The mothers are only able to force a faint smile by thanking the heavens and trusting in good fortune when their daughters have been verified to have virginity by their husbands and verified by both families. Only then do mothers gain the right to flaunt and brag by wearing smiles in their homes. The entire family, the entire race, will hold them in respect. If not, then the family stove of the newly formed home will become cold. Not only will the husband reject her, the father will also turn his mother away, as she had not been able to protect her daughter's chastity. Both families will henceforth become sworn enemies. Gentlemen who have been to or are going to Xinjiang to explore, it is possible that you have not paid attention to the delicate details of the issue of chastity. Now I implore you to understand.

A Woman Cannot Let Others See Her

Let's put aside whether

or not this is fundamentally

a religious issue. The most conservative of Xinjiang's Hui Muslim scholars, the ahongs, advocate the separation of men and women. Women cannot let others see them, except for their husbands. They must cover their faces with veils. They claim such advocacy is rooted in their religious duties. The most fiercely debated and even bloody issue that pits the ahongs against the reformists is the issue of veils. Have you seen an ahong of the Muslim faith ever encounter a woman wearing a veil without averting their eyes? They consider it sinful to look upon a woman. I think this is widely known. If you have not seen such a thing, then you cannot be considered to have visited Xinjiang. Given all of these facts, how could pitiful mothers allow their eleven or twelve-year-old daughters' first night rights to be enjoyed by the ahongs? At the same time, how would ahongs with such conviction ever dare commit such illegal acts? Liars who confuse right and wrong, can we force you to admit the lies, or will you admit it yourselves? The sins of those who fabricate rumours for money have landed upon your heads. Are you even responsible for the lies that you have told?

Islam Forbids Prostitution and Gambling

For a long time now, we have paid attention to the issue of prostitution amongst the Islamic code of laws. What is (haram)? It is to say that matters forbidden by the Lord should be refrained from at all times. For example, one should not eat pork, drink alcohol, or engage in prostitution. Everyone, so long as they are a Muslim or a Muslim child, can understand and obey these tenets. The ahongs teach these values to the people at all times. They must themselves obey the strict laws before they can teach it to others. After these principles have spread throughout society and the people, people have welcomed and accepted them without needing to be asked. This is one of the most important reasons that Islam could so deeply entrench itself within the Turkish race. The Turkish race places great emphasis on protecting chastity under the Islamic code of laws. This concept is deeply compatible with the convictions of the Turkish race. Which race nowadays closes up their grown daughters inside their homes so that strangers may not see them? Which race makes women cover their faces when they go outside? Which race locks their daughters in tightly guarded carts when they travel? Why do they allow foreigners to scold us for being conservative and unliberated? Why do they suffer people's scorn? These are all methods that have been found in order to protect their own chastity. Have any of you who have travelled to Xinjiang seen such things? If you have seen it, have you researched into their causes? Should a scholar of race or of social customs not bring this kind of research to the eyes of the Han Chinese? Do you still expect society to believe your illogical, irrational ramblings which were made to show off? Do you still think that Chinese society is that infantile? Nonsense. (Central News Agency)

Hubei Establishes Tonglin District in Xiangyang

Dividing into Five Zones to Reclaim Over 500,000 Mu of Wasteland

Aiming to Plant 30 Million Tung Trees Within Five Years

Hankou Communication: Tung oil products occupy an important position in China's export surplus. In a time of frequent disasters and economic depression, promoting tung tree planting is especially important for economic construction. Last year's flood in Hubei province caused losses of over half of agricultural products, but the tung oil production was 300,000 dan, worth 5 million taels of silver. The people relied on it to recover from the disaster. As a result, the issue of tung tree planting has attracted widespread attention. The provincial government has already issued an order to the entire province to make widespread tung tree planting the main forestry policy this year. Xiangyang has many uncultivated barren mountains and wasteland, which are very suitable for tung tree planting. The former Administrative Commissioner of the Eighth District, Cheng Zerun, has drafted a plan to establish a large-scale tung forest area in Xiangyang and submitted it to the provincial government for approval. It is planned that all land in the county, except for cultivated land, will be made into a tung forest area. It is estimated that 30 million tung trees will be planted in five years, and after ten years, the annual income will be more than 3 million yuan and less than 30 million yuan. The steps are divided into five years of tung tree planting, carried out during the agricultural off-season in spring and winter each year. In the first year (1936), 6 million trees will be planted (divided into spring and winter). In the second year (1937), the third year (1938), the fourth year (1939), and the fifth year (1940), 6 million trees will be planted each year. The areas will be selected from the barren hills and plains of Xiangyang. In the first year, it is planned to designate the surrounding areas of various temples such as Nanxizao Pond, Guyin Temple, Yanqing Temple, Ganquan Temple, Xianshi Temple, and Wolfo Temple, each with an area of 15-16,000 mu, totaling 100,000 mu, as the first tung forest area in Xiangyang County. In the second year, it is planned to designate the 100,000 mu of long hills from Weishan Mountain and Lumen Temple to Pangju Temple as the second tung forest area. In the third year, it is planned to designate the 100,000 mu of mountains, earth ridges and Bawang Mountain from Wangjiaji to Chenjiaji as the third tung forest area. In the fourth year, it is planned to designate the 100,000 mu of hills near Longzhong as the fourth tung forest area. In the fifth year, it is planned to designate the 100,000 mu of hills in the Wushao Ridge southwest of Baimadong as the fifth tung forest area. The locations of the above tung forest areas are all not far from the Han River, and transportation is quite convenient. This spring, sowing will be carried out at the aforementioned locations first. If there are insufficient numbers, it is planned to select barren land in the Luyan post area of the Sixth District of the county, such as Ganggou, Zhao Gang, Qiaowa, and other places with relatively sloping ridges and poor soil quality, and sow 10,000 mu. It is estimated that 180 tung seeds are needed per mu, which is about one sheng. 100,000 mu will require about 1,000 shi of seeds. 50,000 mu will be sown this spring. Please have the provincial government distribute 500 shi of tung seeds. In the future, 1,000 shi of tung seeds will be prepared each year, which will be sufficient. Regarding the work, each person's daily labor can sow four mu of tung trees. For 100,000 mu, about 25,000 workers are needed, divided into spring and winter, with about 12,500 workers needed each season. With five workdays per person, about 2,500 people are needed, who will be recruited from the nearby strong men in the tung forest area in accordance with the people's labor service regulations. Students from agricultural and forestry experimental schools will be in charge of the guidance work, and some long-term workers will be hired to take charge. As for the 10,000 mu in Luyan Post area, the district agricultural school will be fully responsible. For management personnel, a forest police team will be organized, and officials from the public service agencies in the tung forest area and the abbots of various temples will be dispatched for short-term training, so that they can each return to their original positions to take charge. For the sake of thorough management of the affairs of each forest area, a management committee will be specially established to manage everything. If tung oil seeds are not cultivated after sowing, the development will inevitably decline. It is planned to carry out cultivation twice a year. The first time will be after the sap flows in spring, and the second time will be during the tree's dormancy period. The labor of the two cultivations each year will be undertaken by the security team and the strong men of each bao, which will not violate agricultural time and will also obtain the benefits of production. Long-term cultivation and fertilization will be carried out by the hired long-term forest police. The distribution of other benefits will be discussed and decided by the tung forest management committee, taking into account the harvest situation and the current situation. As for the repayment of the seed money, about 15-16,000 yuan is needed to purchase 1,000 shi of tung seeds each year. Please have the provincial government purchase and distribute it in advance. As for the method of repaying the seed money, it is planned to include 5,000 yuan in the Xiangyang production and construction budget each year to repay a part. On the day the tung seeds are profitable, Chudi will be returned as soon as possible. After tung oil is planted, if the land is suitable, tung oil seeds can be produced after three years. To improve the quality and quantity of tung oil and accelerate the process for the aforementioned large number of tung trees and tung seeds, a new-style mechanical oil mill should be established in the third year. If this oil mill requires a large amount of money, and the county government's production and construction funds are insufficient, a request will be submitted to the provincial government for subsidies, or commercial shares will be solicited for management. (April 13)

Kunshan Strangles Daughter to Death; Father Detained for Legal Action

Lu Jingshi, the head of Zhouxiang Township in the Sixth District of Kunshan County, had a son named Bingyuan, who is currently an elementary school teacher. At around 7:00 p.m. on the 21st of last month, he suddenly slashed his newly born two-month-old daughter's face twice, causing the bridge of her nose to break and blood to flow profusely. Although he was persuaded by others to seek medical treatment, it was ultimately ineffective, and she died on the 16th. The incident was learned of by the police officers of the Public Security Bureau, who immediately detained Jingshi and his son, as well as the child's mother, Ms. Chen, and the judiciary sent personnel to verify the facts and deal with them strictly according to the law.

Bandits Found Again in Suzhou East Tai Lake

Recently, major robbery cases have occurred frequently in the lakeside villages of Wu County. Therefore, the Wu County water and land police and the provincial security team set off on the 14th in seven routes to conduct a joint patrol and suppression. However, the search and suppression yielded nothing. The water and land police teams returned to their respective defenses on the 15th. Unexpectedly, two bandit ships were found near the Xinkai River Maoqi Port in East Tai Lake on the evening of the 16th, carrying more than 20 bandits with firearms. They were spotted by local fishing boats, who stealthily reported to the nearby water and land police. However, when they went to arrest them, the bandit ships had already disappeared. Zhang Hanwei, the director of the Wu County Public Security Bureau, ordered all branch offices in the townships to investigate strictly and arrest the bandits as soon as possible and punish them according to the law to deter the bandits because Chen Muxiang was kidnapped, a ransom was demanded, and Shen Rushen was torn up by the bandits and his body was abandoned near Guanyin Mountain.

Official Police Murder Case Scheduled for Trial

The official police murder case in Guanzai Lane, where the main culprit He Naikang and others refused to accept the death sentence imposed by the local court and appealed to the High Court, has been summoned once. Now the High Court has summoned a large number of relevant witnesses, more than thirty people, and has scheduled a court hearing on the 20th and 21st of this month in two days.

Soybean Cake Merchants in Various Counties Vigorously Fight for Business Tax

Representatives of the oil cake industry from more than ten counties, including Danyang, Wuxi, and Suzhou, held a meeting in Suzhou the other day to vigorously fight for the soybean cake business tax rate. They elected Yu Shengzu and four others as representatives and scheduled to gather in Zhenjiang on the 20th to petition the Provincial Government's Department of Finance, requesting a reduction in the tax rate. The soybean cake industry has always been taxed at a rate of 2/1000, which has now been changed to 5/1000. They still request a reduction to 2/1000 to ease the burden on merchants.

Wuxi Green Town Fish Merchants Suspend Business

Although Qingyang Town is a major town in the Sixth District of Jiangyin County, business is prosperous, but commercial transactions and market prices are all based on news from Wuxi. It is very close to towns such as Shizhuang North Qifang Yeqiao in Xijing, and has a close commercial relationship with Xiyi. It is learned that there was originally a small vegetable market in the town on Dantong Road, but business was not very developed due to its remote location. Later, it was moved to the Majia Field in Beilong for business, but the place was outdoors and there were no houses. If it rained, snowed, or was hot, it could not be sold. Therefore, vegetable vendors complied with the regulations superficially, but fishmongers built buildings and opened fish shops for business on both sides of the Central Bridge. Recently, the town paid attention to cleanliness, and Inspector Ding Jiarong of the Second Public Security Sub-Station was ordered to ban the opening of fish shops in the buildings next to the bridge, and summoned the shop owners Wu Zu'an, Chen Zaiyao, Zang Agou and others one after another, ordering them to close their shops. After people temporarily bailed them out for reconsideration, starting yesterday (the 16th), the town's fish merchants suddenly suspended business uniformly, waiting for a solution.

Nantong Nine Chang Fishing Fleets Set Sail in Large Numbers

Due to the approaching peak season for yellow croaker, fishing boats from the nine coastal Chang areas of Tongshu in Jiangbei set sail in large numbers. There are more than 1,000 fishing boats on the ocean surface in the Shengsi Dongsha fishing areas. The water police escort fleet has now set sail in separate areas. The sea is calm during this fishing season, and the fishing harvest is expected to be very promising.

Bandits in Eastern Township Rampant

Recently, due to the severe spring famine in the Yuxi area of the Eastern Township of Tongyi, bandits took the opportunity to wreak havoc. The families of Ji Jinhua and others were robbed, and many people were injured and killed. The attack team has rushed to suppress the bandits.

Zhenjiang Jiangsu Bank Small Loans

Jiangsu Bank is providing relief to small-scale industrial and commercial businesses by offering small loans for industrial and commercial activities. However, they must be introduced by local industrial and commercial groups. Therefore, applicants for loans must be reviewed and certified by the guild and then transferred to the Chamber of Commerce before they can be granted a loan. The maximum amount is 2,000 yuan, with a term of four months. If the loan is not repaid on time, the guarantor will be held fully responsible. Preparations are now underway, but such loans are difficult to be comprehensive without administrative protection. A request has now been submitted to the provincial government to order all counties to notify industrial and commercial groups to assist. It is also heard that in the future, chambers of commerce in various counties will have to organize a loan review committee to specialize in this matter.

Yangzhou, Villagers from the Western Suburbs Come to the City to Petition

Recently, due to land price issues, hundreds of villagers, including men, women, the old, and the young, from the area of the earthwork project site outside the West Gate of the county gathered on the 16th, each holding a small flag, and came to the city to petition the county government. Subsequently, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang led a team to inform them that the government had already decided on a method regarding the land price that should be given, and they should wait patiently for it to be issued. The villagers, believing that their request had yielded results, then dispersed.

Robbery of a Woman During a Temple Fair

In Caowang Market, a village belonging to this county, during a recent temple fair, Li Longbao, a stonemason and follower of Chen Dengxin, led dozens of people, including Xu Rongchang and Tian Chaoda, and forcibly took He Qiqin's sister back to his home, intending to rape her. The woman refused and sent a message home. Upon hearing the news, the He family, with the help of local guards from both sides, took the woman back. They have filed a lawsuit with the court, accusing them of rape.

Hangzhou, Reduction in Rice Transportation Costs on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau has received a letter from the Zhejiang Construction Department stating that this province is a rice-deficient area, and the food produced is not sufficient for consumption. Now that the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway has been opened to Nanchang, Jiangxi Province has an annual surplus of 2 million dan of rice, which can be transported to Zhejiang to supplement the food supply and regulate food prices. However, due to the high cost of railway transportation, each dan costs 9 jiao. They have requested a reduction in price to benefit the people's food supply. The railway bureau yesterday sent Transportation Section Chief Zeng Shirong to the Construction Department to discuss price reduction methods, which will be implemented after seeking instructions from Director-General Zeng. In addition, the railway bureau, due to the increasing volume of cargo transportation between Nanchang and Hangzhou, has purchased seventy more freight cars to be transported to Hangzhou for use and has allocated 30,000 yuan to build seven warehouses along the line to meet the needs.

Jiaxing, Jiahe Cloth Factory Announces Liquidation

The Jiahe Cloth Factory in Jiaxing's Xihe Street, which has been in operation for more than 30 years, is divided into more than ten departments, including iron looms, wooden looms, dyeing, and refining. During its peak, there were more than 1,000 male and female weavers. The cloth produced was sold in major ports throughout the country, and there was also a distribution office in Shanghai. In recent years, affected by the commercial downturn, sales have been sluggish. Even the retail department has struggled due to weak purchasing power, making it difficult to manage finances. As a result, the factory has suffered significant losses. After a meeting of shareholders yesterday, it was decided to liquidate and close down the factory. Cao Tingrong, Gu Suming, Jiang Laixian, and others were appointed as liquidators. The liquidation process began on the 17th. It is said that wealthy merchants such as Bao Chu and others will take over the factory and continue its operation. However, during this liquidation period, the livelihoods of over 700 weavers will be greatly affected, which is truly pitiful.

The Jiaxing County Government, in accordance with orders to urge the people to pay old taxes, has established a Tax Collection Office and appointed a director to be in charge. Those who delay will be summoned and forced to pay. It is reported that many major households have been summoned and forced to pay. In less than a month since its establishment, the office has collected nearly 100,000 yuan in back taxes, which is a remarkable achievement. The Central Bank Recalls and Destroys Copper Coins and Silver Dimes

After the Ministry of Finance issued new subsidiary coins, it is currently recalling and destroying copper coins and silver dimes. It has ordered the Central Bank to handle this. In addition to purchasing them directly, the bank has also reached an agreement with the city's tram companies and public transportation companies to jointly purchase them at the legal price and send them directly to the Central Mint for storage. It is said that the bank has already collected 500,000 yuan worth of copper coins, totaling 10 million coins. The copper material can be melted down and recast into new coins. However, this matter must be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval.

The Ministry of Finance Specifically Approves Two Banks in Jiangsu Province to Issue New Subsidiary Coin Notes with a Total Value of One Million to Recall Miscellaneous Notes from the Xuzhou Official Exchange Bureau; Preparations Are Underway for the Production and Issuance of One, Two, and Five Jiao Notes

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, recognizing that the jiao notes issued by the Xuzhou Pingshi Official Exchange Bureau are widely circulated in the rural areas of northern Jiangsu, while the counties in southern Jiangsu do not need them and there are discounts when they are circulated, and some refuse to accept them, believes that these jiao notes are hindering the circulation of legal tender. It had intended to request the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications to exchange them for new subsidiary coin notes, but the subsidiary notes printed by these three banks are not sufficient for distribution. Therefore, it specifically consulted the Ministry of Finance to temporarily allow the Jiangsu Bank and Farmers Bank to issue 6 million yuan to recall these miscellaneous notes and regulate the market.

The Ministry of Finance Specifically Approves. The Ministry of Finance, after considering the Jiangsu Province's request, has replied to Jiangsu Province, stating that since the central government is currently minting new subsidiary coins, the requested issuance of 6 million yuan in subsidiary coin notes is too large. Furthermore, since the Xuzhou Pingshi Official Exchange Bureau increased the issuance of jiao notes in 1932, the amount circulating in the counties of northern Jiangsu does not exceed 3 million yuan. The copper coin notes previously issued have also been gradually recalled, so such a large amount is not necessary. For the purpose of recalling miscellaneous notes and regulating the rural economy, the two banks are temporarily allowed to fulfill their obligations and issue 3 million yuan in subsidiary notes. They must pay 40% in cash and 60% in guarantee reserves in accordance with the law. It is also stipulated that when the central government has sufficient new subsidiary coins, they will be recalled and destroyed.

Printing and Issuance Begins. It is learned that the Jiangsu Provincial Bank and Jiangsu Farmers Bank have been ordered to fulfill their respective obligations and begin printing subsidiary notes. The types of subsidiary notes include one jiao, two jiao, and five jiao notes. It is expected that they will begin circulating in the rural areas of Jiangsu Province in early June to recall various miscellaneous notes in order to consolidate the policy of unified currency. The branch offices of the two banks in various counties will have exchange points for Xuzhou official notes. At that time, people can go directly to exchange them.

The Fish Market Officially Transferred Yesterday Morning; Ministry of Finance Specially Sends Secretary Qian Maoxun to Supervise the Inventory; Minister Wu Will Come to Shanghai to Preside Over the Opening Ceremony; Opening Decided for May 1st

After the Shanghai Fish Market Management Committee was established and the general manager and deputy managers were appointed, General Manager Wang Xiaolai went to Beijing twice to meet with Minister Wu for instructions. He returned to Shanghai the night before last and went to the fish market with Director Du Yuesheng and others yesterday morning to take over the market buildings, documents, contracts, and other items. Former Manager Jin Kai Zhan led the staff of various departments to hand over the items. The opening date of the market was decided to be May 1st. Minister Wu will come to Shanghai to preside over the ceremony. Details are as follows:

Mr. Wang Goes to Beijing. When the Fish Market Board of Directors was established, two directors and one supervisor were appointed to handle the takeover with the general manager and deputy managers. At that time, General Manager Wang, because the market was about to open, had to decide on the internal organization and business policies. Therefore, he went to Beijing twice to meet with Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang for instructions. He returned to Shanghai the night before last and went to take over yesterday morning in order to actively prepare for the scheduled opening.

Transfer Method. The personnel who went to receive the market yesterday included Chairman Du Yuesheng, Standing Directors Tingfang, Lin Kanghou, Zhang Fayao, Tang Chengzong, Resident Supervisor Xinzhi, General Manager Gan Xiaolai, Deputy Managers Zhu Kaiguan and Sun Guchen, Accountant Tang Zaizhang, Secretary Li Zizai, and more than ten others. Former Manager Jin Kaizhan invited them to lunch, then led them to inspect the auction hall, wharf, warehouse, cold storage, ice-making room, and other places. They then divided up to hand over the documents and contracts. Ministry of Finance Special Secretary Qian Maoxun supervised the inventory. Du Yuesheng and others left first, while Wang Xiaolai and others left around 4:00 p.m.

Business Philosophy. According to Wang Xiaolai, in an interview with a reporter from the Central News Agency, he went to Beijing twice to meet with Minister Wu to seek instructions on the market's organization and other matters. The fish market is an emerging industry in our country, and since all methods have been changed, the assistance of specialized personnel is required to handle it. The personnel previously dispatched by the Ministry are experts in fisheries, so they will still be relied upon. In terms of personnel, careful consideration will be given. All expenses will also be minimized. Minister Wu greatly appreciated this intention. He also discussed in detail how to reduce commissions to ease the burden on producers and consumers, strive for cleanliness and hygiene of products, provide economic assistance to fishermen to encourage fishing and increase production, so that consumers can obtain inexpensive necessities, and how to deal with the existing fish merchants at the Sixteenth Wharf to ensure they cooperate with the market and do not suffer losses. In short, the Ministry is committed to developing the fishing industry, and he will follow suit to promote its establishment.

Market Building. The fish market is located on the Jiangxinsha in Pudong and is magnificent and well-equipped. The entire building resembles a ship, with the broker's office in the rear, shaped like a semicircle. To the right are the water tower and cold storage. The construction of the walls and the installation of machinery were delayed, so it was completed last. The motors were tested recently, and the results were excellent. The cold storage equipment includes a freezing room with an area of 118.7 square meters and a volume of 392 cubic meters. It has two freezers and cooling pipes, which keep the temperature at -15 degrees Fahrenheit, with a cooling rate of 20,000 B.T.U. per hour. It can freeze 30.5 metric tons of fish in 24 hours. There are five cold storage rooms with a total area of 817.5 square meters and a volume of 2,699.3 cubic meters. The cooling pipes use a direct expansion system to maintain a constant temperature of 0 degrees Fahrenheit, with a cooling rate of 660,000 B.T.U. per hour. It can store 1,500 English tons of fish. The ice-making room has an area of 204.5 square meters and a volume of 965.2 cubic meters. Below it is a water pool with 672 ice containers, covered with wooden lids. Each container can freeze 300 pounds of ice. The daily ice production is 50 tons. Each room has cork-lined walls, with a thickness of 6 to 9 inches, and the doors are sealed with rubber to prevent heat transfer.

Total Construction Costs. The refrigeration for ice-making and cold storage uses an ammonia compression method. The machine room is equipped with two canopies and 5,000 bottles of ammonia to drive all the machines, with a total horsepower of 487. Four ammonia compressors, each powered by 100 horsepower, compress the ammonia liquid into the condenser to cool it and send it to each part, using the heat absorption effect during its expansion to freeze the ice and generate cold air. The water used is drawn from two deep wells, each reaching 550 feet. The power of 10 horsepower is also used to pump water into the storage tank, and after precipitation, it is pumped into the water tower, which has a capacity of 100 tons, to supply drinking water and ice-making for the entire venue. All electricity is supplied by the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, with each machine using 82 degrees of electricity per hour. The entire machine project was undertaken by the Dick Machine Factory at a cost of 350,000 yuan. Including the wharf construction cost of 100,000 yuan, the building construction cost of 280,000 yuan, and the equipment costs for the tracks in the venue, the total cost is 800,000 yuan.

Page 11

Sugar Merchants Affected by Smuggling in North China; National Sugar Enters a Desperate Situation

All Sixteen Sugar Firms in the City Have Suspended Operations; Accumulated Inventory and Few Sales Pose a Risk of Stagnation; Sugar Merchants Telegraph the Ministry of Finance and Various Provinces Seeking Relief

According to the Dihua News Agency, in recent years, the sugar industry in our country has shown significant improvement. In the past, most of the sugar consumed by Chinese people was foreign sugar. In recent years, sugarcane has been widely planted in Guangdong Province, and the output has greatly increased. Therefore, the sales of domestic sugar have surpassed those of foreign sugar. The general management office for sales is located in Shanghai. All domestic and foreign sugar is transferred to various provinces in Central and North China via Shanghai. Therefore, the sales of foreign sugar in Shanghai are almost nationwide. All provinces such as Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Shandong, Hebei, Hubei, Henan, Hunan, Shanxi, and Shaanxi purchase from Shanghai. Therefore, Shanghai is a key transportation hub for the sugar industry, and the annual business volume is also very large, with annual sales of 5 million dan, which, calculated at the current price of 22 yuan per dan, can reach 100 million yuan.

Smuggled Sugar Dumping; Domestic Sugar Disappears

Since last year, the smuggling at the customs in North China has greatly affected our country's sugar industry. Since the first, second, and third months of this year, the large-scale smuggling by Japanese ronin, especially of sugar, has further damaged the domestic sugar industry. Because smuggled sugar has low costs, the selling price is very low, only 15 or 16 yuan per dan. The selling price of domestic sugar is about 22 yuan. As a result, smuggled sugar can be sold smoothly. Initially, it was only in the Tianjin area, but it spread to Shaanxi, Shanxi, Hebei, and other provinces, and then penetrated into Anhui, Henan, Hunan, and other provinces. Recently, even Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have been flooded with smuggled sugar. Domestic sugar has become increasingly unpopular.

Various Provinces in the Interior Suffer the Same Fate

According to Xue Meiting of the city's Sugar Industry Association, all provinces in the interior are now dominated by smuggled sugar. The cost price of this type of sugar is quite balanced, with little fluctuation. At most, it only differs by two or three jiao per dan. If we pay taxes according to regulations, the cost will be more than 20 yuan, making it impossible to lower the price to compete with the 15 or 16 yuan smuggled sugar. As a result, Chinese sugar merchants are suffering terribly. Currently, merchants in various provinces find foreign sugar more profitable. Even those who deal in foreign cloth are now switching to the sugar business. The general invasion of smuggled sugar is evident. Ordinary sugar merchants want to purchase formally sourced sugar, but fear being outcompeted by low-priced smuggled sugar, so they have no choice but to switch to purchasing smuggled sugar. As a result, the provinces no longer deal in domestic sugar.

Damage Reaches Millions

According to the current situation, all 62 sugar firms in the city have suspended operations. Sales are non-existent, business is sluggish, and everyone is in dire straits and on the verge of collapse. The sugar business in the city in the previous month and the month before that only reached 10,000 packages, worth only about 200,000 yuan. If we follow the example of annual business reaching 100 million yuan, then even though these few days are slow days, the sluggishness of the business is evident. Currently, domestic sugar is piled up at the Jinliyuan Wharf, Gonghexiang Wharf, and other places, and there is no way to clear it out.

Telegraph to Authorities Urging Relief

Chinese merchants throughout the city believe that if this continues, the risk of business closure is imminent. Therefore, they telegraphed the Ministry of Finance a few days ago to quickly discuss effective measures, but it is difficult to start. The Sugar Industry Association is currently drafting a telegram to the Finance Department of the Shaanxi Provincial Government, requesting that a special consumption tax be levied on smuggled sugar to make its selling price similar to that of non-smuggled sugar in order to help formal sugar merchants. However, the outcome is difficult to predict. It is hoped that the authorities will quickly formulate fundamental remedies.

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Association, at the invitation of the Zhejiang and Jiangxi provincial governments, is collecting products from various factories to lead participation in the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Special Products Joint Exhibition.
