Sugar Market: Shantou Exchange Rate Increases, Chaozhou Sugar Remains Difficult to Loosen

Regarding domestic Chaozhou sugar, according to reliable news from Shantou, the rumor of Qing sugar being converted to coarse sand is impossible and uncalculated, and such a thing will never happen. However, Shantou still needs to see an increase, with the possibility of reaching 1,200 yuan. Originally, if the exchange rate increases, the market price could be lowered, but the inventory in Shantou is not abundant. If the exchange rate increases, the accumulated price will also rise accordingly, and there is no hope of seeing a decrease for the time being. Therefore, the Shanghai market is gradually tightening. Few merchant's goods are being offered. Yesterday, only a total of 53 bags of Qing sugar were traded at 10.04 USD per bag. There were no further offers. However, miscellaneous white sugar showed signs of downstream demand.

The Public Association's trading panel, such as second-grade coarse sand white, Dong Chi white, and local factory cotton white, called out the original price. There were few buyers and no signs of improvement. However, after the inter-bid, the future market suddenly rose by 5 yuan. If the customs gold tightens today, it may improve slightly.

The Sugar Industry Platform Company held its term for bid exchange yesterday. The total quota was 4,607 bags. The bid price remained unchanged. As a result, a total of 540 bags were traded, including 530 bags of Five Sheep coarse white sugar produced in Guangzhou at 11.85 USD per bag, and 1 bag of No. 4 cotton white sugar at 20.09 USD per bag. The remaining Qu Xi coarse white sugar at 21.65 USD, No. cotton sugar at 21.10 USD, and medium sand white sugar at 20.06 USD were not sold.

Dried Goods: New Season Is Still Far Away, Daylily Market Is Tightening

Daylily: Although the sales of goods from Guangdong are not prosperous, the inventory in the Kui market is ultimately low, and the source is lacking. Therefore, merchant's warehouses are holding back on offering goods, and the trend is tightening. It is heard that the price of Zhenjiang production has also rebounded by about 1 yuan. Yesterday, the Zhenjiang merchant's warehouse quoted a higher price of 27 yuan for better-quality goods. The quoted prices for other Xuzhou daylilies have also increased, and there is no intention to sell urgently. The future market is bound to tighten. The new season is still far away. After a long period of fatigue, there is often a possibility of rebounding.

Seafood: Old Fish Maw Inventory Is Not High

New fish maw will soon be available, but the old goods in the warehouses and the inventory on the street are also running low, so the market situation is extremely stable. However, the purchase of long goods has recently been suspended by foreign firms, and sales are sluggish. Reliance on business from Tianjin, Qingdao, Hankou, and other domestic sources is limited. Therefore, the market is slightly weaker than before. The inventory at the bottom is not high, and prices can still be maintained. Yesterday, brokers offered high-quality long glue at 100 yuan, second-quality at 90 yuan, rootless goods at 110 yuan, Ningbo Zhamian glue at 150 yuan to 140 yuan, Dadao Yuan dried at 135 yuan, general goods at 130 yuan, Waishan tip slice belly at 165 yuan to 160 yuan, Wenzhou goods first grade at 160 yuan, second grade at 140 yuan, Diaopian belly at 120-130 yuan, thick Zhuang rice fish glue at 148 yuan, and Tongshou at 120 yuan.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Firms Traded Slightly

Yesterday, overseas silk prices rebounded slightly, but Shanghai silk prices were small, so transactions with foreign firms have gradually approached. For example, Baichang's June and July futures were resold yesterday. Although the price was slightly weaker, it was still satisfactory. It is estimated that Xinfu Dachang and other firms purchased a total of 35 bales.

Piece Goods: La Seine Flannel Is Selling Well

Yesterday, the market atmosphere at the Wool Fabric Public Welfare Association was very good. There were transactions from both local merchants and customers from other regions. Most of the running street brokers had substantial sales, mostly by check. La Seine flannel is currently selling well. Door merchants and Western clothing merchants all have substantial imports. Yongle's first-grade goods were sold yesterday at a uniform price of 4.95 USD per yard, and Haohua's goods were sold at 3.85 USD, up from the previous day. This is because the foreign firms have run out of stock, and the current market is short of spot goods.

Hardware: Supply and Demand for Large Tinplate Are Balanced

Due to the scarcity of incoming large tinplate, there is a fear of running out of stock. New Taikoo Warehouses have had new goods arriving since the day before yesterday, but the number is limited. Therefore, those who hold the goods continue to hoard them, so prices are very firm. However, the transaction is quite strong, and the goods offered are also quite impressive. The 24-gauge patterned tinplate is selling well due to strong purchases from yarn factories and is also short of stock. Therefore, the standard once rose to 400 yuan. Recently, some have been loaded overseas, and the sales market has slightly loosened, selling for 200 yuan per box. It is estimated that 20 to 30 boxes have been offered in the past two days. Although 26-gauge yarn factories and toy factories also have transactions, the inventory is larger. More than a dozen boxes have been offered, and the most sales are made by hardware stores along North Suzhou Road. Although hardware stores along Bailao Road also have inventory, the asking price is very high, so transactions are slightly quiet.

Miscellaneous: Black and White Pepper Prices Fall

For use in the pharmaceutical industry, produced in Dutch-owned Makassar and other places, the amount imported into our country each year is quite large. In past years, imports have always been over 10,000 dan. Although there was a poor harvest last year, there were still over 8,000 dan. The largest sales markets are Sichuan and Hubei. Demand in the northern provinces is also very common, but customer sales are strongest in the winter. Now, in late spring and early summer, the climate is gradually getting hotter, and business is becoming sparse, so the market is also trending downward. Yesterday, merchant's warehouses offered 40 packages of black pepper at 41.50 yuan, 20 packages of No. 1 pepper at 41 yuan, 17 packages of white pepper, high-quality goods at 78 yuan, and second-quality goods at 70.05 yuan, down 1 yuan from the previous offering. There are few buyers, and the market is extremely weak.

Ordinary Yellow Gardenia Declines

Recently, the arrival of yellow gardenia is occasional, but sales are declining. Therefore, there are few buyers for ordinary goods, and sales are becoming sluggish. Yesterday, it was heard that a batch has been offered, and the quality is still dry, but the color is not good, causing the asking price to fall by nearly 1 yuan compared to the previous offer. However, goods with large grains and good color are still in demand due to low inventory, and the market is expected to remain stable in the future. The arrival and inventory are rare, and the future can be expected to be stable.

Shen Bao Women's Supplement

Consolidating Our Right to Self-Determination

— Lu Gu Wenshu

In the past decade or so, amidst the clash of new and old ideas, our Chinese women's sphere has seen three distinct perspectives on our relationship with ourselves, society, and family.

The first advocates that serving society is more important than managing a household, based on the ideas of 18th-century thinkers like Voltaire, Jean-Jacques Rousseau, Olympe de Gouges, who believed that women are also human beings and should stand on an equal footing with men. Therefore, women should also devote themselves to serving society, considering that a woman's primary function is not merely to raise children and perpetuate the race.

The second argues that family is more important than society, diametrically opposed to the previous view. It suggests that women, due to their physiology or knowledge, are better suited to stay at home, manage household affairs, and educate children, as the Bible says, "A good woman holds the distaff in her hand and does the hardest work." This means fulfilling a woman's natural duty and being a model of a virtuous wife and good mother, without constantly showing her face outside. Furthermore, men governing the outside and women governing the inside perfectly embodies the spirit of human cooperation. Besides, if women always stay at home, it can reduce the number of unemployed people in society, which is very beneficial to society, isn't it?

The third advocates for equal emphasis on serving society and managing a household, encompassing the reasons of the previous two. It believes that if women can value both career and family equally, without distinguishing between them, their status can remain high permanently. At the same time, they won't forget their instincts, neither failing society nor neglecting their family, becoming a perfect woman.

After careful consideration of the above three views, the last one seems the most reasonable and appropriate. However, in reality, it is not easy to achieve, because one person has to take care of both sides. Unlike mothers in Soviet Russia and Germany who can have someone take care of their housework and children while they work outside, this view is only good in theory but not very practical.

As for the first and second views, they seem very different on the surface. However, a study of their core reveals that they are still the same. The core of the first is serving society, and I say that the core of the second is also serving society. Why? Because raising well-behaved children at home is to cultivate them into pure and noble citizens in the future, and isn't this work indirectly serving society?

Therefore, I believe that all these views are correct. We only need to determine the way we serve society, directly or indirectly, based on our own environment, situation, body, temperament, and knowledge. We should not be confined to a certain prejudice, rigidly defining that doing this is right and doing that is wrong, becoming a woman without any autonomy. In short, the most important thing is to know that the right to choose the path of our relationship with society and family belongs to us. We must permanently protect this sacred right of self-determination, and not allow anyone or any force to direct, interfere with, or control it.

The Joys of Singlehood

— Meng Su

Greedy for Freedom... Abandoning Responsibility

I have a friend who is a single woman of thirty-six years old, whose charm has not diminished with age. Her family is middle-class. Her parents are both well-known in the community. She herself has received higher education. In the past few years, she has been pursued by many men in the romantic arena, but she has never fallen into love. In recent years, she has resolutely rejected all proposals and expressed her determination to remain single for the rest of her life. She is now a woman with a noble profession. I have debated with her repeatedly about her stubborn views, hoping that she would change her mind, marry a good husband as soon as possible, and become a virtuous wife and good mother of the new era. However, her eloquence was unimpeded, and she rejected my advice outright. Summarizing her views, there are many wonderful remarks as follows:

"Freedom is the most beautiful truth in the world. People are born for freedom and die for freedom. Among women, only unmarried women can truly enjoy freedom and happiness."

"I am willing to fully enjoy freedom during my lifetime, and I am unwilling to sell my innate freedom at any price..."

"I make a living myself, freely choose my profession, and freely associate with my friends, unlike married women who are restrained by their husbands' preferences. I can avoid insincere socializing because of the people my husband loves. I can do whatever I want with everything in the world. When I love quiet, I can be alone without the disturbance of children. If I want children to accompany me, I can choose one from the orphanage and touch her."

"Because I am an unmarried woman, and my appearance is not below average, almost every man who sees me expresses obvious willingness to get close. I only allow them to be my spiritual friends. This may not be enough to be proud of."

"My sisters of the same age are now wives or mothers of a group of children. Every time they meet me, they always talk about my life and future. They even hold infinite worries for me, as if they see me as a lonely boat in the sea, not knowing where it will drift; as if they see me as a lost lamb, sooner or later to be swallowed by wild jackals. As for me, I am indifferent to their well-intentioned overthinking. I cannot understand where the happiness of marriage lies. I regard myself as a vast wild goose, soaring freely to the east, west, south, and north; going up and down in all directions as I please. Why shouldn't I enjoy my own beauty for a long time!..."

I express infinite admiration and great regret for this self-admiring modern "Bei Gong Ying'er." Freedom is indeed precious. But how can marriage deprive a woman of her entire freedom? There are indeed many discordant couples in the world, but there are also many harmonious couples. If you are afraid of falling into the forest of discordant couples and remain single for a long time, how is that different from giving up eating for fear of choking? The joy of family among loving couples, how can it be dreamed of by those who bitterly adhere to singlehood! Even putting aside the calculation of joy and suffering, the male and female bodies of human beings are predetermined by nature, and there is a joint responsibility to be borne.

In ancient times, Bei Gong Ying'er removed her earrings and ornaments and did not marry until old age in order to support her parents. How could parents be willing to make their daughters spend their lives as widows in order to entertain themselves in their old age? Therefore, this kind of filial piety has long become a thing of the past; moreover, merely for personal freedom, to lightly cast off the responsibility that should be borne for the nation, how is that different from a soldier deserting before battle! Although the law does not prohibit people from being single, it also cannot be justified on the grounds of moral law.

Ugly Women and Crime

— Hui Fang

In the position of social life, beautiful women and ugly women each have different attitudes. A beauty with a bad fate often feels that the happiness of an ugly woman is an unnatural state and harbors dissatisfaction. As for an ugly woman who has suffered misfortune, she feels that this encounter is entirely caused by her ugliness, and she feels depressed and unhappy.

All ugly women are mostly "sexually weak," so they often try to use strengths other than appearance to make up for the shortcomings of ugliness; such as performing arts, skills, decoration, wealth, etc., which can achieve this goal in many situations. Moreover, ugly women are mostly not as arrogant as beautiful women. The so-called "ugly woman's deep affection" is also the reason for this. However, the ugly woman's awareness of being a "sexually inferior person" can never be eliminated by the above-mentioned supplements, and its influence on her daily life is deeply rooted. Therefore, it has a considerable relationship with crime.

According to those who handle fat crime cases, the number of ugly women who commit adultery is high. Although this cannot be said to be an entirely credible fact, there is also a suitable reason for it. Because ugly women lack the attention and contact of men, it is not easy to obtain the enthusiasm of men, as with many beautiful women. Once a man treats her sincerely, according to common sense, she is very likely to have great pleasure and feel sexual satisfaction. This is the major reason that drives ugly women closer to crime. Women who often lack interaction with the opposite sex and are estranged from each other will never easily let go of this opportunity when they unexpectedly obtain this opportunity, causing them to lose their discretion and consideration, and sacrifice their chastity. There is also a saying that although there are also many beautiful women who commit adultery, compared with the adultery of ugly women, there is a great difference. Because the husband of a beautiful woman, even if he finds out that his wife has committed adultery, he may deliberately hide the matter for fear of losing this beautiful woman. On the contrary, if a woman who has an affair is an ugly woman, then her husband has already been more alienated from her on weekdays, and at this time, he will have less forgiveness, and therefore expose her ugly behavior. According to the numbers, the fact that ugly women commit adultery with others more often may be a superficial phenomenon. This theory also seems to have its own point of view.

Furthermore, because ugly women are not easy to obtain the love of the opposite sex, when they occupy the opposite sex, they must do their best to cater to them, making every effort to please them, pouring all their love and goodwill on their opponents. Once they are abandoned by their opponents, or their opponents are taken away by others, they will inevitably experience intense emotions such as jealousy, anger, and resentment, which is very different from the coldness of beautiful women towards the opposite sex. Because she wants to avenge the hatred of this "sexual failure," an abandoned woman can commit crimes such as arson and murder. A close examination of such items disclosed in the daily headlines shows that ugly women are in the majority. This kind of hatred can also be vented by committing adultery with others. There are also cases where a woman is abandoned by her husband, leading her to become self-abandoned, resulting in crimes. Or, embarrassed by the difficulty of life, they commit adultery with others in order to seek reliance, or obtain money, and engage in prostitution. (This article is based on Kenkichi Ichijima's "Marriage and Crime")

The Actual Situation of French Women's Lives

— Qiu Wen

When we talk about the prosperity of Paris, we often associate it with the romance, extravagance, and debauchery of the women there. All of this is enough to symbolize that they are not a country of a high-class people. However, those who have actually been to the whole of France know that French women also have to work hard at the productive work they should be responsible for, and no one is willing to waste the whole day in enjoyment. Although they regard entertainment and decoration as their second life besides work, we know that the people of any country should be given adequate time for rest and entertainment besides work.

French women are probably less involved in national institutions because they do not have the right to vote. Almost all of them seek development in commerce. In the business fields and shops of any city or town, female employees account for six out of ten. As for entertainment venues (including cinemas, dance halls, and cafes), they are completely run by women. For the sake of business transactions, they inevitably have opportunities to come into contact with male customers, which creates the spark for their romance. Moreover, in their country, it is not a big deal for a woman to marry seven or eight times. Society does not add any contempt or discrimination to them.

As for women in the fields and villages, they are even more honest, simple, and hardworking than those in the cities. In spring and autumn, women in the fields get up every day before dawn (which is about 4:00 AM in our country), the whole family has to get up, hurriedly eat breakfast, and then the family has to work in the fields with hoes and plows until sunset before returning home to rest. As for women working in factories, they also work eight hours a day, starting work at 6:00 AM, stopping work at 10:00 AM, starting work at 12:00 PM, and stopping work at 4:00 PM. It is not like our country, which adopts a night work system, because their national women's association has a regulation that "the night belongs to all of us women." Although many women are willing to increase night work for the sake of livelihood, once the state finds out, the factory will be punished by the state.

Another thing worth mentioning is that married women in France should bear a great responsibility. When children reach school age, mothers have to send them to school for a considerable education. Only after the state has tested them and passed them after a certain number of years can mothers be completely relieved of their responsibilities. Therefore, only a small number of women with children are still serving in society. Otherwise, they are entrusted to an agency specializing in managing student education (there is no specific term for this there, but these places are very common, somewhat like nurseries in the Soviet Union.) However, as mothers, they still have to constantly undertake the educational duties of supervising and correcting.

Their most common entertainment venue is the coffee shop established in every city, town, and village because the dance halls in the city require great architecture and magnificent equipment. People in the countryside and fields do not need these because the coffee shops there are not just eateries like in our country, but also places where they can dance and have fun. They open at 7:00 PM every night, and then men and women come here one after another, but they stop at 10:00 PM. Their entertainment program is only drinking a cup of coffee and dancing a few times, and there are absolutely no excessive actions.

From the above brief report on the lives of French women, we know that they are also an advancing nation, and like Soviet women, they have to work hard for the country's production. They are definitely not like our country's women who spend the whole day engaging in a life of pleasure.

Losing One's Temper

— Shijiu

Nine out of ten Chinese women suffer from liver qi disease. It is said that when liver qi attacks, a lump of qi pushes upward from the chest, and the patient groans and writhes in great pain. It is said that Xi Shi clutching her chest in pain was probably due to an attack of liver qi. There is no specific medicine for treating liver qi. Many patients have told me that just taking a puff of opium will make the qi lump in the chest disappear. I don't know if this is drinking poison to quench thirst, and it has ruined many people!

Old-fashioned women often develop liver qi disease because of discord between husband and wife, discord between mother-in-law and daughter-in-law, or because they have suffered other anger. Mrs. Zhao envied vanity when she was young, and her youth was wasted. Later, she married a wealthy opium addict, thinking that she could finally be satisfied. Who knew that her husband would marry a concubine, and from then on, quarrels and disputes between husband and wife were often heard, and she developed liver qi disease. Fortunately, smoking was convenient, so she became inextricably linked with opium, and every time she met someone with the same disease, she would praise the miraculous effect of opium, and respectfully give it to others to smoke, beautifully calling it "a fragrant puff."

Mrs. Han is her neighbor. That lady has a belly as big as a five-stone gourd, and it is said that she also suffers from liver qi disease. The reason for her illness was due to a sentence from her mother-in-law. Once, she suffered from dystocia, and everyone else was anxious, but her mother-in-law sneered, "Others can give birth and raise children quickly, only you..." Mrs. Han got angry when she heard this, and she got liver qi disease. One day, the two ladies met, and they first talked about some trivial household matters, and then they talked about the problem of liver qi disease, and Mrs. Zhao wanted to persuade Mrs. Han to take "a fragrant puff" again. Mrs. Han was afraid of being scolded by her husband, so she finally did not dare to take a puff; however, sympathizing with each other, it is difficult for Mrs. Han to guarantee that she will not follow in Mrs. Zhao's footsteps!

Chinese women have always been good at worrying and prone to illness: worrying is nothing more than being subjected to qi stagnation; and nine out of ten diseases are probably liver qi disease. However, opium can eliminate the qi lump in the chest; therefore, I especially cite the above facts to persuade the ladies in the family not to be fooled by it again.

Women of Qinghai

— Yu Lin

Qinghai is in the west of China. The people there build tents as houses. A stove is set up in the tent, and the tent is divided into two parts. The left part is for men, and the right part is for women. They think it is a shameful thing for husband and wife to sleep in the same place.

There is no distinction between men and women in Qinghai. Anyone who has been to Qinghai will definitely see many young men and women holding guns and riding horses to hunt wild animals in the mountains and fields.

Every morning, women in Qinghai drive livestock into the mountains to graze, and at noon, they milk cows and sheep. In the afternoon, they are at home doing things such as fetching water, twisting wool, washing clothes, and making sour milk, gum milk, milk residue, milk cakes, milk butter, milk powder, and milk rice. In addition to the above things, women do, other things such as sewing clothes and shooting guns to catch thieves are all the responsibility of the men.

Women's clothes are all made of silk, and their coats are all made of animal skins. The sleeves of the clothes they wear only reach below the wrist, and the waist is very tight. The skirts they wear are very long and tight all around because they do not wear pants all year round. They do not wash themselves all year round, and even when they wash, they only use a teacup to hold water and dab it. Their hair is braided into hundreds of braids, and a cloth is attached to the braids, about five inches wide, all the way to the heel, and silver ornaments and agate stones are hung on it. Poor people also have copper stones hanging on them, weighing several pounds. The earrings are as big as our bracelets, and some even add two strings of coral, hanging on the shoulders, as a beauty.

Special Feature from this Newspaper

Mrs. Shao Yuanchong, Ms. Zhang Mojun, on Women's Issues

— Ji Ping

Ms. Zhang Mojun is one of the leaders of women's suffrage in China, and the reporter has long admired her. During this tour of the capital, I was introduced by Dr. Zhu Junyi and had the pleasure of meeting her. The lady is graceful in appearance, but her words and deeds are dignified and upright, worthy of being a heroine. Everything she discusses should be regarded as a model by the women's community. The following is a record of the conversation:

What are the things worth remembering from your time as a student?

"When I was studying, there were three things worth remembering: (1) When I was young, I studied at Wuben Girls' Middle School in Shanghai between the years of Jia Chen and Bing Wu. At that time, I had already joined the Tongmenghui and engaged in the revolutionary movement; at that time, the Qing court's search and arrest were very strict, so my actions were extremely secretive. One day, Principal Wu Huaijiu summoned me to the office and asked, "Why did you join the Tongmenghui and engage in revolutionary work?" I knew that he had read my correspondence and discovered it, so I replied, "The Manchus, as a foreign race, have entered the Central Plains and implemented autocratic tyranny, oppressing our nation and shackling our people's intelligence; making it impossible for our nation to develop and the national power to decline day by day. All of us Han people should rise up and join the Tongmenghui, unite as one, and overthrow the foreign government." Wu said, "This matter is extremely dangerous! In case it is discovered in the future, be careful not to implicate the school." I said sternly, "A man who undertakes a task dares to act and dare to bear the responsibility. If I do something, I should bear the responsibility myself and never implicate others." Wu smiled when he heard this and said, "How brave you are, young man!" (2) One day, a woman came to the school to visit me. It happened that I was out, and when I returned, the schoolboy told me, "A woman in a kimono came to visit just now. She didn't say her name, but left a note." I looked at the note, which said: "I am returning to the country for important matters, and will return gradually in a few days. I would like to contact you first. I didn't meet you at the moment and didn't wait long. I am disappointed!" Below was signed a "Qiu" character. When I saw this character, I knew that she was my comrade Qiu Jin. At that time, because I didn't know her address, I couldn't return the visit, which was very disappointing. Not long after, I heard that she was martyred in Zhejiang. I regretted very much that I didn't go with her at that time to shed blood for the nation together, and I was unhappy for months. (3) Once, Wuben Girls' School held a school-wide sports meeting. There was an item called "Race with Flags." The teacher ordered me to write on four pieces of cloth of several feet square in the midst of a crowd. I immediately waved the four large characters "I Jianwu Jie," which were in the Northern Wei style, which is different from my current calligraphy. At that time, newspapers made versions and published them. This was also taking advantage of the momentary excitement to show the promotion of the martial spirit of our nation. Thinking back to my childhood, there is a lingering taste."

Please recall the social undertakings you have created in the past.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Essays

Relieving Schooling Loss and Reducing Tuition Fees

— Xing An

Under our country's aristocratic education system, it is extremely difficult for young people to receive education. The high fees charged by schools at all levels are often beyond the means of ordinary people. As a result, only children from wealthy families have the opportunity to attend school, while children from ordinary families suffer from the hardship of not being able to afford education. Given the recent decline in the national economy, the number of young people who have lost the opportunity to attend school has only increased. This situation is extremely serious, not only for the individual misfortune of young people, but also for the loss to society and the nation!

Recently, in order to alleviate the loss of schooling for young people, the Ministry of Education submitted a proposal to the Executive Yuan, ordering all public and private schools across the country to set up free and publicly funded places from this year onwards as follows: Free places, A. Elementary schools should in principle not charge tuition fees. The implementation of this principle should be strictly examined and supervised. Even those that still charge fees should be ordered to gradually increase the number of free places; B. Secondary schools and higher vocational schools should set up at least 5% or more of the total number of students as free places; Publicly funded places should be set at 2% to 4% of the total number of students. This is an excellent approach, although the scope of relief is limited; however, at least some poor students can gain more opportunities to study. We hope that the principle of free tuition in elementary schools can be implemented as soon as possible so that compulsory education can be universally promoted. The number of free and publicly funded places in secondary and higher vocational schools should also be increased year by year so that those who cannot afford to study are not excluded from schools.

However, we believe that in order to alleviate the loss of schooling for young people, it is important to set up free and publicly funded places, but it is also urgent to order schools at all levels to reduce all fees. The former can only reward a small number of outstanding students with good character and academics who cannot afford to study, while the latter can reduce the burden on most student families. In our country's schools, in addition to tuition, board, and books, there are also fees for clothing, lectures, and physical education: there are truly many items that are difficult to list. Other extractions such as registration, admission, and compensation fees are unbearable. Therefore, we hope that the education authorities should pay attention to this point and find ways to improve it. In addition to setting a maximum tuition fee for schools at all levels, all improper fees must be abolished. In this way, a group of young people can have more opportunities to study. This is also a problem that cannot be ignored in alleviating the loss of schooling.

Storm

— Lao Xin

——A Story of Maritime Navigation——

The sky was so gloomy it felt like it was about to collapse. Strange gusts of wind blew across the Pearl River from time to time, causing people's hearts to tremble. Several foreign warships anchored on the Bai'etan sea across the river were all fired up. Their fat, sturdy smokestacks emitted thick plumes of black smoke, as if waiting for something. Anyone who had traveled on the inland river knew that this ominous weather was not a good sign, but for some reason, our cargo ship was about to set sail again from Guangzhou, heading up the Xijiang River. Everyone was unhappy, working listlessly as if unwilling.

"Damn your ancestors' stinky mouths…hurrying? Hurrying to Zhaoqing to send someone off to their death?"

Fifth Uncle cursed under his breath as he untied the mooring ropes. Third Elder was also gloomy-faced today, lacking any energy. He simply reiterated the Second Boss's instructions as usual, like a megaphone—

"This time, we'll be fine after unloading the goods in Zhaoqing. But we need to hurry. It's the seventh day of the month today, and we need to get to Zhaoqing by the eleventh. The return trip will be easy, so let's all put in a little more effort!"

He himself was the number one person lacking energy. The long pipe leaned against his knee, and he was too lazy to strike a match to light the bag of Old Farmer brand tobacco he had already packed. Even his eyelids were too tired to lift. He looked like someone who had been exhausted for seven or eight days, neither human nor ghost. Not to mention Old Seven, Zhang Tiebi from the Chenghuang Temple had told him earlier on shore that his luck was bad and he should beware of villains. He had been worrying about it ever since. Taking advantage of Old Gui's brief respite, he asked in a low voice:

"Can you guarantee a safe trip this time? Look—they've hoisted the typhoon warning!"

He pointed to the frightening typhoon warning indicating a hurricane was approaching the province. Old Gui ignored him, but Third Elder frowned and remained silent.

Rumors were spreading from the small steamer in front: It's not good to set sail today!

"It's the tail end of a wind coming from Hong Kong. This trip won't be easy. Who can guarantee nothing will happen?"

"Isn't that right? Jue Wei Long's rebellion is no joke. They say he'll turn a few somersaults in the sky, and the whole world will change!"

"We have to go! Everything is ready. If you're too cowardly to be afraid of death, we'll call someone else."

A cargo ship next door was also rushing goods to Wuzhou, and they were even more eager than us. We were all thinking: It doesn't matter whether we go or not. We're just working for them, and it's not our responsibility whether we make it on time. On the contrary, we were hoping for a big storm so we could hide in the provincial capital for a few days of fun…

Woo…

The long, mournful sound of the small steamer's whistle shattered our hopes. It was slowly starting to move, towing us three cargo ships that weren't willing to risk our lives, away from the docks. By this time, Bai'etan had turned into one or two small mountains. The wind stirred up waves, and the wind was mixed with a layer of yellow sand, making the river surface murky and difficult to navigate. The small steamer was risking its life. The somewhat reluctant and mournful whistle sounded like a funeral dirge. Everyone who heard it felt a pang in their hearts.

Old Seven stared blankly at me, wrinkles furrowing his brow. His nostrils were pinched with fright, and his lips were pale as if someone had pinched them. Sweat was beading on his forehead and the tip of his nose. His eyes were unfocused, as if saying helplessly: We're at the mercy of fate! A gust of wind slapped him in the face, and waves splashed all over him. His hair was soaked with water, and his skin was covered in goosebumps. At this time, I was also like a fool, my mind empty, yet wanting to think about everything. Old Gui and Fifth Uncle were working hard, putting in their best effort, because they were the most experienced. Third Elder was useless, as old as a chicken coop with no use.

The wind grew stronger and stronger. A few drops, unsure whether they were spray or rain, landed on us, causing us to shiver. The sky was getting so dark it looked like the world was truly about to change. The situation was already very bad. Someone next door was shouting hoarsely:

"Take cover! Take cover! You're risking the lives of your eighteen generations of ancestors! Take cover at Baixian Shell nearby! Hey, we're cutting the cables!…"

The ship sailed out of Bai'etan, and the sea was vast and empty, making it even harder to navigate. The ship was rocking like a baby's cradle. One of the cargo ships had broken its cable and was drifting backwards. We didn't know what to do. Third Elder, who was usually very calm, was also at a loss.

"Ah, ai—wa!…"

Followed by several chaotic screams, the small steamer in front had hit something. People were constantly calling for help. Then the towing cable jerked us violently. The ship tilted to one side, and half the hold was filled with water. The raindrops were falling thicker and thicker, stinging like arrows hitting our bodies. But we couldn't worry about that. Taking buckets, Old Seven and I hurriedly scooped water out. But somehow, before we could stabilize the ship, a warship with a white flag and a red sun on it suddenly rammed into us diagonally, causing waves that made our cargo ship even more unstable—

"Save—"

The terrifying scream was not completed before Fifth Uncle fell into the water as the ship tilted to the right. Old

Page 20

Gui calmly grabbed a thick cabin plank and jumped into the water, swimming vigorously towards where Fifth Uncle had fallen. But the waves were huge. I anxiously watched as Old Gui hadn't reached him yet, and Fifth Uncle struggled twice before disappearing from sight. Third Elder next to me sighed deeply. The place where we were standing was also unstable. The ship was completely overturned.

On the roaring sea, I clung to a wooden box, enduring a long, endless night under the onslaught of wind and rain.

Nocturne

— Liang Qiyun

I remember when the flowers bloom.

However, for me, that is now a flowing stream of the past.

The pavement after the light rain seemed a little muddy.

We walked along the moat.

The moat was full, carrying some withered vegetable petals and green grass slowly away.

Across the river at the bottom, the ancient mountain city outlined rough contours in the dim light of the night, so quiet. It was like an old man harboring contempt for the hearts of young people, and at the same time feeling the sadness of his impending demise, so he lay there helplessly, silently watching the sky. —The dark sky, no moon, a few stars timidly revealing pale, bitter smiles...

Due to my habitual night walks, I was familiar with my shadow. In the past, seeing that in addition to myself, there was also a slender, tall companion, I felt that everything was gentle and affectionate.

Shadows are always silent. We had passed many days in silence.

Now, it's gone! Both are monotonous and clumsy.

"Too lonely," I sighed.

Looking forward, in a place almost obscured by distance, there were forests spreading like mist, and behind the forests, high mountain shadows erected like curtains, the mountain soil, and a slender tower stood tall. It was a pity that it was night, otherwise, I would definitely run there to see if flowers were blooming everywhere. Has March in early spring really arrived? Why does the wind today still carry a cold chill!

"Young people shouldn't be like this." Minjun, my fellow traveler, my preacher, began our debate again. —Every time, every time, our arguments always concluded with his smug, triumphant laughter, and my boundless resentment. —He continued, "Losing a woman's love is not such a big deal. What's the point of being so melancholy! Other people, who have lost their homes, who have lost their countries, aren't they all about to cry themselves to death?"

The hateful preacher's face shook, shook in front of me. My chest suddenly filled with anger, regret, and annoyance. What use is this practically empty theory to me! I really don't want to pay attention to him. However, for the sake of getting angry, I quickly replied:

"This is my own business!"

"Yes, I know that... Then, what do you want to do?"

"What do I want to do? What can I do! Just endure the pain."

"'Endurance' is the worst thing!" he said contemptuously.

"Not necessarily. Under certain conditions, there is a minimum limit, endure as much as possible. —I believe this is reasonable."

"Ah, fool, you are completely wrong! Because—this is precisely 'a symptom of the submission of the weak.' No, no, you should—"

He almost shouted it out.

"But, think about it, even a dead volcano has a day of resurrection. What's more…" —Although I felt I had the right to add this sentence; at the same time, I also knew that this would not help the facts.

"No, you should straighten your chest immediately!"

"Yes, there will be such a day."

I smiled. Turning my head to look at him, he was also smiling.

So, we were silent...

After walking this straight pavement and turning into a narrower, muddier alley, I leaned over to his ear and said:

"Even dead volcanoes have a day of resurrection! Look, friend."

I remember when the flowers bloom.

I also remember when the flowers fall.

However, for me, is this really becoming a flowing stream of the past?

No, there is still sunshine tomorrow.

In Front of the Temple of the Martial Saint

— Zhi Fu

In the morning, a large crowd surrounded the Temple of the Martial Saint, crowding the front gate so tightly that not a drop of water could pass through. People stretched their necks, their gazes all focused on the brand new black-lettered announcement with a red circle around it.

"Oh! Repairing the Wanyuan Bridge!..." someone who could read shouted.

Then, those who had squeezed in returned, which generally would not elicit public agreement! People's faces, previously happy, now seemed to have an extra layer of displeasure. In that displeased expression, millions of complaints were about to burst out from everyone's hearts.

"In such a barren year, building a bridge, isn't it clearly wanting to take..." Zhou Datou was afraid of raising his voice too high, so he stopped there. Looking back, luckily, he hadn't been seen by the boss. He paused before adding the word "money" to complete the sentence, sticking out his tongue, making a face, and shrinking back under the shed.

..."Repairing the bridge doesn't really count as doing good deeds! If they have money, giving out rice... giving out porridge... that counts as accumulating merit!" Qian Laizi said those words well, clenched his left hand, and punched the air, hoping the crowd would praise him and give him a cheer.

"I'll never walk on that damned bridge in my life, I don't care about the accounting!" Then Zhou Datou added fiercely. After speaking, he turned around and ran east.

"Damn it! Wasn't it the last time they built that Daming Temple that Little Tumor Lord made a fortune..." Hong Ajiu, who was sitting on the stone lion, was drunk again today and talking nonsense:

"Good! Throw it away..." Qian Laizi kept up his efforts, preparing to fabricate a reason to defeat him.

Then, people were agitated, and most agreed with Laizi's words.

Cursing and shouting mixed together. Hong Ajiu, with some drunkenness, took the lead in rushing into the crowd and tearing down the paper, throwing it at his feet.

"Ah! Trouble is brewing! In front of the Temple of the Martial Saint, chaos has begun. Some are running with their heads in their hands, like dogs splashed with hot oil.

Gradually... someone ran to inform Tumor Lord of this bad news. He opened his eyes wide. He didn't even button up his jacket and casually took three tough guys with him, rushing to the temple. The flesh on his face was horizontal. One would suspect he was a hound who would immediately devour all the small animals...

"Humph! Building the bridge is my idea, who dares to make trouble! I'll make sure they suffer..." Tumor Lord panted, making threatening gestures to the crowd, his bright eyes targeting Hong Ajiu's entire body.

Hong Ajiu continued with his drunkenness, his angry expression undiminished, raising his thick eyebrows, showing his intention to retaliate against Tumor Lord, but in a flash, the three tough guys seemed to have understood the intention, rushed over and grabbed the drunkard, very easily.

Struggling was useless. Hong Ajiu's steps began to stagger, and white foam appeared on the corner of his mouth, like a lamb waiting to be slaughtered.

"Trouble! Ajiu has caused trouble..." The crowd did not go to help, only this weak cry, it was impossible to discern who said it.

The bridge still had to be built. Hong Ajiu was treated as the culprit and sent to the station.

Movie

Silver Jottings

— Yun Er

At the end of last year, someone initiated a grand celebration for three couples living together. At that time, no fewer than fifty or sixty people signed up to join, but somehow, this matter was cancelled invisibly.

Recently, I got an unbelievable but reliable piece of news, saying that three couples living together will hold a group wedding at the Lassus Dance School on the afternoon of the 20th.

The previously rumored three couples were Xu Xingzhi, Chen Luming, Tang Na, Lan Ping, Zhao Dan, and Ye Luxi. And now, the couples holding the group wedding, except for the latter two couples remaining the same, the first couple has changed to Gu Eryi and Lulu's younger sister.

Their wedding ceremony is very unique, probably involving the three couples jointly performing a play.

After the wedding ceremony, a dance will follow in the evening. Fortunately, everything is readily available at Lassus.

This piece of news seems very unbelievable, but the source of the news is very reliable, and it probably isn't someone playing a joke.

After the three couples, what is unforgettable is also "Tiger" Zheng Junxing. If Junxing takes his Miss Huang along, then he can very well join in a cameo performance. The reason for the cameo could be as a practice "best man" for the wedding, as a friend joining in the congratulations, or even as ××. Isn't that right, Miss Huang and my Tiger's "friendship" is rumored to be very "mature"?

Boris Karloff Stars in "The Invisible Avenger"
